Q: What are the keyboard controls?
A: You can view the keyboard controls by pressing F1. Press F1 again to make them go away.
Q: How do I take a screenshot?
A: Press F12 and the screenshot will be saved in the ScreenShot folder in your Sky-Fighter install directory as SF_#####.png.
Q: How do I view the map?
A: Press M or F4 and you'll see the map. Your position is the orange cursor, while your formation members are in green and arena members in blue. Their names will appear by their arrows.
Q: Why doesn't booster work?
A: If your capacity is over 70%, fuel consumption is doubled. If it's over 80%, you can't use boost. If it's over 90%, you'll only be able to move at minimum speed. To increase your gear's capacity, either equip a CPU with fuel or spend skill points on fuel.
Q: What is fuel?
A: Fuel is indicated on left top side, above energy/shield gauge, and when fuel is consumed, you can buy it at city supply shop or at the landing site. When you run out of fuel, you crash.
Q: How do I use the MP3 player?
A: Copy your mp3 files into the Music folder in your Sky-Fighter install directory. Then in game, click on the arrow up button and you'll be able to view your songs and select how they're played. (randomly, in order, repeating, and so on) All controls are similar to those on a CD player, and if you hilight a song and press DELETE, that song will be removed from your playlist. You may also set the player to play from a different directory. Click on "MUSIC" while in town and it'll prompt you to choose a play directory.
Q: How can I modify/share this FAQ?
A: Look for FAQ_Main.txt in your Sky-Fighter install directory and follow the file's pattern, questions with Q followed by a colon, and answers with A followed b a colon. Once you put in your own questions/answers and then upload the file to a fansite. Keep in mind that fan-made FAQ files are not officially supported by Sky-Fighter. 
Q: How do you land?
A: Slow down by the Supply Pad, or stop in midair above it, and then press C or \ to land.
Q: What is the inventory window for?
A: This window simply lets you equip different items and change weapons. You can also drag consumable items into your hotkey bar so you can use them faster.
Q: Why is my fuel being used up quickly?
A: If your capacity is over 70%, fuel consumption will double.
Q: Why am I moving so slowly?
A: If your capacity is over 90%, you will only be able to move at minimum speed.
Q: What is an adhesive?
A: There's two types of adhesives. Left adhesives, which go in the slot below the radar, are for items that permanently modify a stat. Right adhesives, which go below the engine, are timed items that increase a stat or perform some special function.
Q: How do I increase my capacity?
A: Put on a fuel CPU or increase your fuel stat. The fuel adhesive will not help with your capacity.
Q: What are the gamble enchant probabilites?
A: Gamble (Prefix/Suffix) enchants can not fail,
Q: What are the weapon and armor enchant probabilities
A: Your first five enchants can not fail, but after 5, there's an increasing chance that the enchant will fail.
Q: What are the engine and radar enchant probabilities
A: All radar and engine enchants can fail; even the first one.
Q: What happens when enchanting fails?
A: The card and weapon/armor disappears. If you use the Enchant item destruction prevention card and it fails, you will only lose enchants over 5.
Q: How do I use skills?
A: While stopped or in city, press V or F6, and then click on "Skill". Drag your skills into the hotbar on the bottom, below your EXP bar. You can use those skills by pressing the corresponding key. A skill in slot 1 is used by pressing "1", and so on. You can only use skills if you have enough SP to use them.
Q: My game crashes/slows down!
A: Make sure your computer's requirements are suitable for Sky-Fighter. Also make sure the "Min Frame" option is on. You may also want to play with the low settings on. 
Q: What happens when my character dies?
A: If you're killed by a monster or a crash, you'll lose SPI. If you don't have enough SPI to lose, you'll lose a percentage of EXP. If you're killed by a player or an enemy nation's defenses, you don't lose anything.
Q: How do I request a duel?
A: You can alt-click their name and select 1:1 battle, or you can press F3 and enter their name. If a player does not wish to duel, do not pester them.
Q: How do I block PvP requests?
A: Type /refusefight in the console to reject PvP requests.
Q: How do I block trades?
A: Type /refusetrade in the console to reject trade requests.
Q: How do I whisper/reply?
A: To whisper to another player, type "<name> message. For example: "Joe Hello! If you type " while whispering with someone, it will automatically enter the name of the last player you contacted/who contacted you.
Q: How do I speak to everyone in a map/in my nation/in my formation/in my brigade?
A: To chat with everyone in the map, type !message. For example: !Hello! To chat with everyone in your nation, type ^message. For example: ^Hello! To chat with everyone in your formation, type #message. To chat with everyone in your brigade, type @message. You must be level 20+ to use $ chat.
Q: What are some level requirements?
A: Trade chat: level 20. Brigade creation: level 20. Duels: level 20. Ments: level 30.
Q: What is a ment?
A: A ment is a message that appears by a player's name. For example, you may see something like: <Character Name>: Welcome to Sky-Fighter! To set a ment, type "/ment <message>".  You must be level 30 before you can use /ment
Q: How do you use colors in chat?
A: Type \ followed by the first letter in a color. \\w\ww is \wWhite\w, \\a\aa is \aAqua\a, etc.
Q: How do I combine items?
A: Go to the factory, put the ingredients in, and click "Combine". This FAQ lists a number of recipes.
Q: Combining vs. enchanting.
A: Combining items in the factory allows you to make new or improved items. Enchanting items in the Laboratory allows you to improve items by adding prefixes, suffixes, enchants, and trails. If you combine an enchanted item with more than one other item, your enchants are lost.
Q: How do I enchant?
A: Go to the Laboratory and put in the item and the card you wish to use to enchant.
Q: What is a rare item?
A: Rare items are green items with a prefix, suffix, or both. You can combine clean weapons with gamble cards to add a fix, or you can find rare items from normal monsters.
Q: What is a unique item?
A: Unique items appear in \yyellow\y and are typically more powerful than normal items. Unique items cannot be enchanted or gambled.
Q: How do I create/delete a brigade?
A: To create a brigade, you must first make a formation. Once you do, go to the Brigade tap and click "Create". Choose a name and if it's accepted, your brigade is born. To delete your brigade, click on "Deploy". It takes one week to delete your brigade, so think carefully before creating a new brigade.
Q: How do I create a formation?
A: Press F7, make sure you're on the Formation tab, and then click "Create". Formations can have up to 10 people and they have various benefits, including formation flying and exp/spi/drop rate bonuses.
Q: How do I set the formation style?
A: You must be the formation leader. In the formation window, there's a list you can choose on the bottom by "FORMATION" button. If it's Free/F, all players must fly around on their own. If it's anything else, players can form up with the form leader by pressing F2. (must be close enough)
Q: How do I set my brigade logo?
A: There's many ways to do it. This is the easiest way that'll work regardless of where your Ace directory is. Keep in mind, you may only set the brigade's logo if you're the brigade's leader. First, go into MS Paint. Next, go to the Image menu, then Attributes. Next, set width to 24, height to 12. Next, draw your logo. Pressing ctrl-pagedown will make it easier for you to draw the logo. (everything will appear 4x as big) Next, ress CTRL-S to save. Don't change any of the settings, and save it as C:\_brigade.bmp. Next, launch Sky-Fighter. Go into the brigade menu. Click on MARK. Next, type in the following EXACTLY as typed here: C:/brigade.bmp (note how the slash is "/" here, but "\" in step 5) and click Accept. Your brigade logo will be set, but it won't be visible immediately.
Q: I can't find my skill. I just bought it. Where is it?
A: Press F6 and go to your Skill tab. There is a scrollbar on the right side. Scroll down, and you'll find the skill.
Q: How do I increase my stats?
A: Press F6 and go to the INFO tab. If you have points, you can raise your stats. Keep in mind, the stats you start with at level 1 reflects the number of points that one stat point will raise the stat by. If your agility starts at 1, you will only get 1 agility for that stat point. If your agility starts at 4, however, your agility will go up 4 per stat point.
Q: How do I start a formation fight?
A: Enter in /formfight followed by the enemy form leader's name. For example, Joe and Bob have a form. Joe would type: /formfight Bob
Q: What is a brigade fight?
A: A brigade fight is simply a fight between two brigades. To use it, type /brigfight [enemy brigade name]. So if Joe is in brigade "Winners" and Bob is in brigade "Losers", Joe would type: /brigfight Losers
Q: How do I reload my missiles?
A: If you've run out of missiles, go to any supply shop to refill them.
Q: How do I search for missions in this FAQ?
A: You can search for missions with the mission level or name.
Q: What are the requirements for the Enrollment test mission/level 1?
A: Go to stones ruin and bring back 3 [Killmarks of bombing exerciser] and 1 [Killmarks of fighter exerciser.] You can see this information on the top-right corner of your screen.
Q: What are the requirements for the Watcher hunting mission/level 2?
A: Bring back 2 overwatcher and 5 watcher computer boxes. You can see this information on the top-right corner of your screen.
Q: What are the requirements for the Petra nest mission/level 3?
A: Bring back 2 Hornian Egg DNA samples from Petra's cave and safely pass through to the end of the cave. You can see this information on the top-right corner of your screen.
Q: What are the requirements for the Bonebat collector mission/level 4?
A: Bring back 7 [gastric juice pockets of bonebat] by bringing down [Bonebats] in Stones ruin. You can see this information on the top-right corner of your screen.
Q: What are the requirements for the Shrine's lookout mission/level 5?
A: Take down monster named superwatcher and bring back its record data. You can see this information on the top-right corner of your screen.
Q: What are the requirements for the Trouble in cave mission/level 6?
A: Go through petra's cave without dying. You can see this information on the top-right corner of your screen.
Q: What are the requirements for the Tylent jungle mission/level 7?
A: Take down Natings, Hornians, Titanmoths and bring back the items that they drop. You can see this information on the top-right corner of your screen.
Q: What are the requirements for the Whisper of angel or devil mission/level 8?
A: Collect as many electric emission devices as you can in 5 minutes. You can see this information on the top-right corner of your screen.
Q: What are the requirements for the Cold hearted muzzle mission/level 9?
A: Take down enemy fighter (I-GEAR EARLY TYPE) that is infiltrating the north of the jungle. You can see this information on the top-right corner of your screen.
Q: What are the requirements for the Buzzing sound mission/level 10?
A: Bring back 8 samples of Hornian DNA, 5 samples of Hornian blazer DNA, and 2 samples of Hornian guardian DNA. You can see this information on the top-right corner of your screen.
Q: What are the requirements for the Decision mission/level 11?
A: It's a simple mission, yet a difficult choice. Choose between the following nations: BCU or ANI. Once you choose a naiton, you cannot switch back.
Q: What is the maximum stat value?
A: 300 is the maximum. Even CPU's will be unable to make stats go over 300.
Q: How do gamble initialization cards work?
A: Go to the Laboratory and put in an item with a prefix/suffix and the corresponding initialization card. The prefix/suffix will be removed.
Q: How does the Enchant item destruct prevention card work?
A: With enchants after 5, if you enchant successfully, you lose the card and gain the enchant. If your enchant fails, you lose the card AND ALL PREVIOUS ENCHANTS EXCEPT YOUR FIRST 5. You still keep your item and its fixes.
Q: How do the brigade cards work?
A: The leader must double-click them to increase the capacity of their brigade. Currently not implemented.
Q: How does the Character Name Change Card work?
A: Leave your formation then double-click the card. Enter a new name and you'll be logged off. Your name should now be changed.
Q: What are "fixes"?
A: "fixes" are prefixes and suffixes.
Q: What are the contested areas?
A: The contested areas are special areas that are only opened to the last nation that took down the enemy mothership. Two nations cannot both have access to the contested areas.
Q: What are motherships?
A: Motherships are the nation's flagships. The ANI mothership is called "\cHoros\c", and the BCU mothership is called "\eAnubis\e".
Q: [Leader only] How do I send nationwide messages?
A: Type: *message
Q: [Leader only] How do I communicate with the other leader(s)?
A: Just whisper to them like you would with any member of your nation.
Q: [Leader only] How do I add notices to the board?
A: The command is /noticeboard [minutes] [message]. Example: /noticeboard 60 Raid at 5pm PST. (posts message to noticeboard for one hour)
Q: Are there any bonuses for killing a nation leader?
A: Currently, no.
Q: Why can't I find the monster to kill to complete my mission?
A: You may not be in the mission map. To make sure you're in the correct map, return to town and then use the "Warp to Mission Map" button.
Q: This mission is too hard!
A: Get someone to help.
Q: There's a mission where I'm supposed to get an item from a monster. I've killed many of them and it still hasn't dropped.
A: Keep trying. Some of these missions have low drop rates, or you're just unlucky. Also, make sure your inventory is not full!
Q: Why can't I trade with someone?
A: You can only trade someone once you have selected a Nation.
Q: Why is this person's name green?
A: Players with green names are nation leaders. They are NOT game staff. They cannot help you with gameplay issues. They simply lead the nation into raids, and work out diplomatic issues with other nations.
Q: When can I start killing enemy players?
A: If you're in BCU, you can travel almost anywhere after completing the level 20 "Reckless Courage" mission. If you're in ANI, you can do the same after completing the level 22 "Rock Elimination Plan" mission. You can fight players before those levels if they enter your territory, but those players are usually extremely powerful. Beware.
Q: How do I buy items from the item shop?
A: You need to purchase Cash Points (CP) from our website to buy these items. Occasionally, we will host events that award Cash Points.
Q: How can I make a shop?
A: First, you must be level 12. Next, you must purchase the "Purchasing Shop" and "Selling Shop" skills from the Skill Shop. They're only 10 SPI each. After that, go to the Bazaar and activate the appropriate skill. You cannot create a shop while in a Formation (including a Formation containing only yourself).
Q: How does Selling Shop work?
A: Simply activate the skill, then drag your items into the selling window. Set a price and quantity (if applicable), then click "Set". Repeat for all your sale items. Finally, set a name for your shop(must be done last) and click "Start". When you click "Stop", the shop will close.
Q: How does Purchasing Shop work?
A: Simply activate the skill. You will be able to browse through the item database so-to-speak and make buying requests. Set an offer price and quantity (if applicable), then click "Set". Repeat for all your desired items. Finally, set a name for your shop(must be done last) and click "Start". When you click "Stop", the shop will close. Please note that equipment with enchantments or 'fixes can not be purchased via the Purchasing Shop.

Q: How do I create a [Garuda Veil Ver. 5] ?
A: Combine 1 [Garuda Veil Ver. 4], 60 [Iron], 60 [Titanium], 60 [Cadmium], and 40 [Strong Moissanite] at the Factory NPC. A 311048 SPI fee will be charged.
